/bin/zsh -lc "git show HEAD:crates/nmp-testing/bin/ffi-stress/common.rs | nl -ba | sed -n '1,80p'" in /Users/pablofernandez/Work/nostr-multi-platform
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	//! ffi-stress — FFI hardening stress harness (M10.5 phase 1).
     2	//!
     3	//! Drives the `nmp_app_*` C symbols via extern declarations (same ABI Swift
     4	//! uses) and verifies S1–S5 gate conditions from
     5	//! `docs/design/ffi-hardening/gates.md`.
     6	//!
     7	//! Usage:
     8	//!   ffi-stress <scenario> [--duration <D>] [--threads <N>] [--fail-on-gate]
     9	//!                         [--write-report]
    10	//!
    11	//! Scenarios: mount-unmount (S1) | dispatch-flood (S2) | snapshot-pressure (S3)
    12	//!            | reconciler-backpressure (S4) | reentrancy (S5)
    13	//!
    14	//! See `docs/design/ffi-hardening/harness.md` §1.2 for the full CLI reference.
    15	
    16	mod allocator;
    17	mod common;
    18	mod ffi;
    19	mod gate;
    20	mod report;
    21	mod s1_mount_unmount;
    22	mod s2_dispatch_flood;
    23	mod s3_snapshot_pressure;
    24	mod s4_reconciler_backpressure;
    25	mod s5_reentrancy;
    26	
    27	use report::{now_unix_seconds, write_scenario_report, ScenarioMetrics};
    28	use std::process;
    29	use std::time::Duration;
    30	
    31	fn main() {
    32	    let args: Vec<String> = std::env::args().collect();
    33	    let cli = match Cli::parse(&args[1..]) {
    34	        Ok(cli) => cli,
    35	        Err(msg) => {
    36	            eprintln!("ffi-stress: {msg}");
    37	            eprintln!("{USAGE}");
    38	            process::exit(1);
    39	        }
    40	    };
    41	
    42	    let mut overall_pass = true;
    43	
    44	    for scenario in &cli.scenarios {
    45	        let mut metrics = ScenarioMetrics::new(scenario_name(scenario));
    46	        metrics.started_at_unix = now_unix_seconds();
    47	
    48	        eprintln!("ffi-stress: running {} …", scenario_name(scenario));
    49	
    50	        match scenario {
    51	            Scenario::MountUnmount => {
    52	                let cfg = s1_mount_unmount::S1Config {
    53	                    duration: cli.duration,
    54	                    ..Default::default()
    55	                };
    56	                s1_mount_unmount::run(cfg, &mut metrics);
    57	            }
    58	            Scenario::DispatchFlood => {
    59	                let cfg = s2_dispatch_flood::S2Config {
    60	                    duration: cli.duration,
    61	                    threads: cli.threads,
    62	                    ..Default::default()
    63	                };
    64	                s2_dispatch_flood::run(cfg, &mut metrics);
    65	            }
    66	            Scenario::SnapshotPressure => {
    67	                let cfg = s3_snapshot_pressure::S3Config::default();
    68	                s3_snapshot_pressure::run(cfg, &mut metrics);
    69	            }
    70	            Scenario::ReconcilerBackpressure => {
    71	                let cfg = s4_reconciler_backpressure::S4Config {
    72	                    duration: cli.duration,
    73	                    ..Default::default()
    74	                };
    75	                s4_reconciler_backpressure::run(cfg, &mut metrics);
    76	            }
    77	            Scenario::Reentrancy => {
    78	                let cfg = s5_reentrancy::S5Config {
    79	                    duration: cli.duration,
    80	                    ..Default::default()
    81	                };

    83	            }

   112	        );

     1	//! Shared helpers used across S3/S4/S5 stress scenarios.
     2	
     3	use crate::ffi::{nmp_app_configure, nmp_app_inject_events, NmpApp};
     4	use std::ffi::CString;
     5	use std::time::Duration;
     6	
     7	/// Inject `count` synthetic timeline events into the kernel via the
     8	/// `nmp_app_inject_events` FFI symbol (test-support only).
     9	///
    10	/// Blocks until the inject command has been enqueued (fire-and-forget per
    11	/// bible #3 — the actor processes them asynchronously).  Callers that need
    12	/// events to be visible before the next emit should insert a short sleep or
    13	/// trigger a `nmp_app_configure` call to force an emit tick.
    14	pub(crate) fn inject_events(app: *mut NmpApp, prefix: &str, base_ts: u64, count: u32) {
    15	    let prefix_cstr = CString::new(prefix).expect("prefix has no interior nuls");
    16	    nmp_app_inject_events(app, prefix_cstr.as_ptr(), base_ts, count);
    17	}
    18	
    19	/// Trigger `configure` to force an emit tick and wait `settle_ms` for the
    20	/// actor to process the event batch and fire the update callback.
    21	pub(crate) fn configure_and_settle(app: *mut NmpApp, settle_ms: u64) {
    22	    nmp_app_configure(app, 0, 500, 12);
    23	    std::thread::sleep(Duration::from_millis(settle_ms));
    24	}
    25	
    26	/// Extract the `"rev":N` field from a JSON byte slice without a full parse.
    27	pub(crate) fn extract_rev(bytes: &[u8]) -> Option<u64> {
    28	    let s = std::str::from_utf8(bytes).ok()?;
    29	    let key = "\"rev\":";
    30	    let pos = s.find(key)?;
    31	    let rest = &s[pos + key.len()..];
    32	    let end = rest.find([',', '}', ' ', '\n']).unwrap_or(rest.len());
    33	    rest[..end].trim().parse::<u64>().ok()
    34	}
    35	
    36	/// Return `true` if the non-zero elements of `revs` are strictly increasing.
    37	pub(crate) fn revs_strictly_increasing(revs: &[u64]) -> bool {
    38	    let non_zero: Vec<u64> = revs.iter().copied().filter(|&r| r > 0).collect();
    39	    if non_zero.len() < 2 {
    40	        return true;
    41	    }
    42	    non_zero.windows(2).all(|w| w[1] > w[0])
    43	}
    44	
    45	/// Return the `pct`-th percentile of a pre-sorted slice.
    46	pub(crate) fn percentile_u64(sorted: &[u64], pct: usize) -> u64 {
    47	    if sorted.is_empty() {
    48	        return 0;
    49	    }
    50	    let idx = ((sorted.len() - 1) * pct) / 100;
    51	    sorted[idx]
    52	}

    52	/// Write `metrics.json` and `report.md` to `docs/perf/m10.5/<scenario>/`.
    53	///
    54	/// The directory name is the scenario prefix (e.g. `S1`, `S2`) extracted from
    55	/// the full scenario name like `S1-mount-unmount`.  Per `ci.md` the bundle path
    56	/// is `docs/perf/m10.5/S1/{metrics.json,report.md}`, not `S1_MOUNT_UNMOUNT`.
    57	pub(crate) fn write_scenario_report(metrics: &ScenarioMetrics) -> io::Result<()> {
    58	    // Extract the leading token before the first '-' and uppercase it.
    59	    // "S1-mount-unmount" -> "S1", "S2-dispatch-flood" -> "S2", etc.
    60	    let scenario_prefix = metrics
    61	        .scenario
    62	        .split('-')
    63	        .next()
    64	        .unwrap_or(&metrics.scenario)
    65	        .to_uppercase();
    66	    let dir = PathBuf::from(format!("docs/perf/m10.5/{scenario_prefix}"));
    67	    fs::create_dir_all(&dir)?;
    68	
    69	    fs::write(
    70	        dir.join("metrics.json"),
    71	        serde_json::to_string_pretty(metrics).expect("serialize metrics"),
    72	    )?;
    73	
    74	    fs::write(dir.join("report.md"), markdown_report(metrics))?;
    75	    Ok(())
    76	}
    77	
    78	fn markdown_report(m: &ScenarioMetrics) -> String {
    79	    let overall = if m.passed { "PASS" } else { "FAIL" };
    80	    let pass_count = m.gates.iter().filter(|g| g.passed).count();
    81	    let total = m.gates.len();
    82	    let mut out = String::new();
    83	
    84	    out.push_str(&format!(
    85	        "# {} — ffi-stress — {}\n\n",
    86	        m.scenario.to_uppercase(),
    87	        iso_date(m.started_at_unix)
    88	    ));
    89	    out.push_str(&format!(
    90	        "- **Tool:** `{}`\n- **Wall time:** {:.1} s\n- **Overall:** **{overall}** ({pass_count}/{total} gates green)\n\n",
    91	        m.tool, m.wall_seconds
    92	    ));
    93	
    94	    out.push_str("## Gates\n\n");
    95	    out.push_str("| Gate | Threshold | Measured | Result |\n");

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	//! Gate checker per `docs/design/ffi-hardening/gates.md` G-S1..G-S5.
     2	//!
     3	//! A `Gate` is a named assertion: measured value op threshold.
     4	//! Collect gates into a `Vec<Gate>` during a scenario run, then call
     5	//! `Gate::all_pass` to determine whether the scenario passed the
     6	//! numeric exit criteria.
     7	//!
     8	//! D6: any gate failure is surfaced here as structured data, not as an
     9	//! opaque error string, so the caller can report, aggregate, and diff.
    10	
    11	use serde::Serialize;
    12	
    13	/// Operator for a gate comparison.
    14	#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Serialize)]
    15	pub(crate) enum GateOp {
    16	    /// `measured <= threshold`
    17	    #[serde(rename = "<=")]
    18	    Lte,
    19	    /// `measured >= threshold`
    20	    #[serde(rename = ">=")]
    21	    Gte,
    22	    /// `measured == threshold`
    23	    #[serde(rename = "==")]
    24	    Eq,
    25	}
    26	
    27	/// One numeric assertion from the gate table.
    28	#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize)]
    29	pub(crate) struct Gate {
    30	    pub(crate) name: String,
    31	    pub(crate) op: GateOp,
    32	    pub(crate) threshold: f64,
    33	    pub(crate) measured: f64,
    34	    pub(crate) passed: bool,
    35	    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]
    36	    pub(crate) note: Option<String>,
    37	}
    38	
    39	impl Gate {
    40	    pub(crate) fn lte(name: impl Into<String>, measured: f64, threshold: f64) -> Self {
    41	        let passed = measured <= threshold;
    42	        Gate {
    43	            name: name.into(),
    44	            op: GateOp::Lte,
    45	            threshold,
    46	            measured,
    47	            passed,
    48	            note: None,
    49	        }
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    pub(crate) fn gte(name: impl Into<String>, measured: f64, threshold: f64) -> Self {
    53	        let passed = measured >= threshold;
    54	        Gate {
    55	            name: name.into(),
    56	            op: GateOp::Gte,
    57	            threshold,
    58	            measured,
    59	            passed,
    60	            note: None,
    61	        }
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    pub(crate) fn eq(name: impl Into<String>, measured: f64, threshold: f64) -> Self {
    65	        let passed = (measured - threshold).abs() < f64::EPSILON;
    66	        Gate {
    67	            name: name.into(),
    68	            op: GateOp::Eq,
    69	            threshold,
    70	            measured,
    71	            passed,
    72	            note: None,
    73	        }
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    pub(crate) fn with_note(mut self, note: impl Into<String>) -> Self {
    77	        self.note = Some(note.into());
    78	        self
    79	    }
    80	
    81	    pub(crate) fn all_pass(gates: &[Gate]) -> bool {
    82	        gates.iter().all(|g| g.passed)
    83	    }
    84	}
    85	
    86	/// Markdown row for one gate. Used by `report::markdown_gates_table`.
    87	impl Gate {
    88	    pub(crate) fn markdown_row(&self) -> String {
    89	        let result = if self.passed { "PASS" } else { "FAIL" };
    90	        let op_str = match self.op {
    91	            GateOp::Lte => "<=",
    92	            GateOp::Gte => ">=",
    93	            GateOp::Eq => "==",
    94	        };
    95	        let note = self
    96	            .note
    97	            .as_deref()
    98	            .map(|n| format!(" ({n})"))
    99	            .unwrap_or_default();
   100	        format!(
   101	            "| {} | {} {:.4} | {:.4} | {} |{}\n",
   102	            self.name, op_str, self.threshold, self.measured, result, note
   103	        )
   104	    }
   105	}

codex
Not fine. I reviewed the requested target `8660961`; master moved to `19411d5` during review, outside this wave.

Findings:
- `8660961` `crates/nmp-testing/bin/ffi-stress/s3_snapshot_pressure.rs:60`, `s4_reconciler_backpressure.rs:63`, `s5_reentrancy.rs:95`: S3/S4/S5 inject synthetic events into the read cache, not `VerifiedEvent` + `EventStore::insert`. `crates/nmp-core/src/kernel/mod.rs:427` writes directly to `self.events`. Fix: create signed/valid events and route through the normal verify/store ingest path.
- `8660961` `crates/nmp-testing/bin/ffi-stress/s1_mount_unmount.rs:117`, `s2_dispatch_flood.rs:154`, `s3_snapshot_pressure.rs:72`, `s4_reconciler_backpressure.rs:160`: gates are not enforced per `gates.md`. Examples: S1 uses 60% not 90%; S2 uses 98% not 600k/100%; S3 uses 1k not 100k; S4 stale-rev/apply gates are missing or hardcoded. Fix: gate exact spec metrics or fail as unobservable.
- `8660961` `crates/nmp-testing/bin/ffi-stress/s5_reentrancy.rs:55`: watchdog timing is broken. `Instant::now().elapsed()` is ~0, so a hung callback may leave `entry_ms == return_ms` and never trip. Fix: use a shared monotonic start or real timestamp plus explicit in-flight state.
- `7e8f607` `crates/nmp-core/src/kernel/ingest.rs:172`: `verify_and_persist()` result is ignored for kind 3/10002 local cache updates. A store-superseded kind:3 can still overwrite `seed_contacts` at `ingest.rs:249`. Fix: gate local cache mutation on `Inserted/Replaced` or derive from store.
- `f7fd6cd` `crates/nmp-core/src/planner/compiler/partition.rs:85`: partition split claim is false. No `case_a/b/c/d` or `inbox_helper` modules exist; `partition.rs` is 353 LOC. Fix: split the claimed modules; keep each under 300 LOC.
